311.7(1): legs bsgrigs byas te/ rje smra seng bla ma'i gsung gi byin rlabs las 'phos pa/ g.yung 
311.8(1): drung bon gyi rgyud gzhung rin po che'i khrod kyi thun mong min pa'i brda chad/[ <<]gsung rab 
311.9(1): sgo mdzod rin po che'i glegs bam[>>]zhes pa dpe tshogs spyi chings kyi mtshan du gsol nas 
311.10(1): dpar 'grems zhus pa yin/
311.11(1): zhus dag thad las rim dngos la thog ma'i ma dpe gang la byas pa/ bar du dpe cha 
311.12(1): gang du bsdur ba/ bsdur ba'i legs cha gang zhig thon pa sogs glegs bam so so'i nang 
311.13(1): dang mjug gi zhus bsgrigs gsal bshad du bris yod/ mdor na nged las mi yongs 
311.14(1): kyis spyi lo 2 11lo nas bzung mi lo lnga yi ring dad pa dag snang dang rang gi dge sbyor 
311.15(1): dang bstan la zhabs phyi gtso bzung thog deb rer tshar grangs bco lnga nas nyi shu bar 
311.16(1): zhus dag byas yod pas sngar las lhag pa'i legs cha zhig thon yod pa'i re ba yod/ 'on 
311.17(1): kyang re 'ga' ma dpe gcig ma gtogs bsdur ya ma rnyed pa dang / re 'ga' bsdur ya 
311.18(1): du ma rnyed kyang bris pa'i chad lhag sogs kyis gcig mtshungs med pa dang / nged zhus 
311.19(1): sgrig pa tsho'i mkhyen dpyod tshad brgal can min pa bcas dang rjes 'gro byas pas nor 
311.20(1): 'khrul gyis bslad pa'ang yod nges pas/ rjes gzigs mkhan rnam pas su dang gang la 
311.21(1): khag dkri med pa rang bstan rang skyong gi 'gan 'khri gtsang ma phrag tu khur ste bstan pa 
311.22(1): rin po che'i ched du nor 'khrul yo bsrang dag ther gnang ba'i skul ma zhu rgyu dang /
312.1(1): mthar don du nged [<<]g.yung drung bon gyi bka' brten dpe rnying phyogs bsgrigs khang [>>]
312.2(1): gis las don rlabs chen 'di 'dra zhig legs grub byung ba ni/ rig gzhung 'di dang 
312.3(1): bstan pa 'di la lhag bsam can gyis phyar gru mnyam 'degs byas pa las byung ba 
312.4(1): yin/ kan su'u mi rigs dpe skrun khang gi dbu khrid 'brug rgyal mkhar dang gcod pa 
312.5(1): rnam gnyis nas thugs khur rgyab skyor tshad med gnang ba dang / lhag par du dus rab 
312.6(1): kyi gnyan 'phrang mang po'i nang tshe srog 'ben dang bsdos te srung skyong byas pa'i dpe cha 
312.7(1): g.yar ba'i dpe bdag rnam pa dang / de bzhin nga tsho'i bstan don gyi bya ba kun la 
312.8(1): mthun sbyor gnang ba ma tshad dpe tshogs 'di dpar skrun skabs su yang ma bskul dang 
312.9(1): blang gis zhal 'debs gnang mkhan bcas dngos shugs brgyud gsum nas rgyu tshegs 
312.10(1): thabs gsum gyis sdong grogs rogs ram gnang mkhan yongs la snying dbus nas 
312.11(1): thugs rje che zhu rgyu dang / gsung rab dag bzhengs byas pa'i dge ba'i tshogs 'dis/
312.12(1): 7 skyabs rje rgyal ba sman ri ba'i mkhan slob rnam gnyis gtsos ris su ma chad pa'i 
312.13(1): bstan 'dzin skyes chen dam pa rnams kyi sku tshe bskal brgyar brtan zhing bzhed dgongs 
312.14(1): lhun gyis 'grub pa dang / 'brel thogs kyi sbyin pa'i bdag po dang las gzhi 'di'i byed 
312.15(1): po kun tshe bsod dbang khams gong nas gong du mtho ste myur du sku gsum rdzogs pa'i 
312.16(1): sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang thob pa dang / zhang bod rig gzhung rnams mi nyams gong nas 
312.17(1): gong du 'phel te 'dzam gling tha gru yongs kyi snod bcud rgud pa gso zhing phan bde'i 
312.18(1): gsos su khyab pa dang / yangs pa'i rgyal khams kun du nad mug 'khrug rtsod dang rang 
312.19(1): byung 'byung ba'i 'jigs pa rnams rmeng med du zhi nas bde legs phun tshogs skyid kyi nyi
